I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
`.env` file is no longer auto-imported
### Describe the bug

After updating `wxt` from `0.20.20` to `0.20.21`, this error is caused:

> Error: Missing required config: CHROME_EXTENSION_ID, FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID

I have these environment variables defined in the `.env` file.

This is probably caused by https://github.com/wxt-dev/wxt/pull/2181

```diff
- import { config } from 'dotenv';
```

Simply importing `dotenv/config` auto-imports the `.env` file. From the [README](https://github.com/motdotla/dotenv#readme):

> ```ts
> // index.js
> require('dotenv').config()
> // or import 'dotenv/config' // for esm
> 
> console.log(`Hello ${process.env.HELLO}`)
> ```
> 
> That's it. `process.env` now has the keys and values you defined in your `.env` file.

### Reproduction

- https://github.com/hyunbinseo/better-surf/releases/tag/v0.0.28
- https://github.com/hyunbinseo/better-surf/actions/runs/24392573474/job/71242144892

_No response_

     3	import { expand } from 'dotenv-expand';
     4	import type { TargetBrowser } from '../../types';
     5	
     6	/** Load environment files based on the current mode and browser. */
     7	export function loadEnv(mode: string, browser: TargetBrowser) {
     8	  const envFiles = [
     9	    // List is ordered with general files first, specific ones last, so the more
    10	    // specific files override the more general ones in the loop below.
    11	    `.env`,
    12	    `.env.local`,
    13	    `.env.${mode}`,
    14	    `.env.${mode}.local`,
    15	    `.env.${browser}`,
    16	    `.env.${browser}.local`,
    17	    `.env.${mode}.${browser}`,
    18	    `.env.${mode}.${browser}.local`,
    19	  ];
    20	
    21	  const parsed = Object.fromEntries<string>(
    22	    envFiles.flatMap((filePath) => {
    23	      if (!existsSync(filePath)) return [];
    24	
    25	      try {
    26	        const content = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
    27	        const parsedEnv = parseEnv(content);
    28	        return Object.entries(parsedEnv) as [string, string][];
    29	      } catch {
    30	        return [];
    31	      }
    32	    }),
    33	  );
    34	
    35	  // Make a copy of `process.env` so that `dotenv-expand` doesn't re-assign the
    36	  // expanded values to the global `process.env`.
    37	  const processEnv = { ...process.env } as Record<string, string>;
    38	
    39	  expand({
    40	    parsed,
    41	    processEnv,
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  return parsed;
    45	}
    46

    36	 *
    37	 * Inline config always has priority over user config. Cli flags are passed as
    38	 * inline config if set. If unset, undefined is passed in, letting this function

    40	 */
    41	export async function resolveConfig(
    42	  inlineConfig: InlineConfig,
    43	  command: WxtCommand,
    44	): Promise<ResolvedConfig> {

    46

    54	    });

    56	    userConfigMetadata = metadata;
    57	  }

    72	    throw new Error(

     4	//#region src/core/utils/env.ts
     5	/** Load environment files based on the current mode and browser. */
     6	function loadEnv(mode, browser) {
     7	        const envFiles = [
     8	                `.env`,
     9	                `.env.local`,
    10	                `.env.${mode}`,
    11	                `.env.${mode}.local`,
    12	                `.env.${browser}`,
    13	                `.env.${browser}.local`,

    16	        ];
    17	        const parsed = Object.fromEntries(envFiles.flatMap((filePath) => {
    18	                if (!existsSync(filePath)) return [];
    19	                try {
    20	                        const parsedEnv = parseEnv(readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8"));

    22	                } catch {
    23	                        return [];
    24	                }
    25	        }));
    26	        expand({
    27	                parsed,
    28	                processEnv: { ...process.env }
    29	        });
    30	        return parsed;
    31	}

     1	'use strict'
     2	
     3	function _resolveEscapeSequences (value) {
     4	  return value.replace(/\\\$/g, '$')
     5	}
     6	
     7	function expandValue (value, processEnv, runningParsed) {
     8	  const env = { ...runningParsed, ...processEnv } // process.env wins
     9	
    10	  const regex = /(?<!\\)\${([^{}]+)}|(?<!\\)\$([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)/g
    11	
    12	  let result = value
    13	  let match
    14	  const seen = new Set() // self-referential checker
    15	
    16	  while ((match = regex.exec(result)) !== null) {
    17	    seen.add(result)
    18	
    19	    const [template, bracedExpression, unbracedExpression] = match
    20	    const expression = bracedExpression || unbracedExpression
    21	
    22	    // match the operators `:+`, `+`, `:-`, and `-`
    23	    const opRegex = /(:\+|\+|:-|-)/
    24	    // find first match
    25	    const opMatch = expression.match(opRegex)
    26	    const splitter = opMatch ? opMatch[0] : null
    27	
    28	    const r = expression.split(splitter)
    29	
    30	    let defaultValue
    31	    let value
    32	
    33	    const key = r.shift()
    34	
    35	    if ([':+', '+'].includes(splitter)) {
    36	      defaultValue = env[key] ? r.join(splitter) : ''
    37	      value = null
    38	    } else {
    39	      defaultValue = r.join(splitter)
    40	      value = env[key]
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    if (value) {
    44	      // self-referential check
    45	      if (seen.has(value)) {
    46	        result = result.replace(template, defaultValue)
    47	      } else {
    48	        result = result.replace(template, value)
    49	      }
    50	    } else {
    51	      result = result.replace(template, defaultValue)
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    // if the result equaled what was in process.env and runningParsed then stop expanding
    55	    if (result === runningParsed[key]) {
    56	      break
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    regex.lastIndex = 0 // reset regex search position to re-evaluate after each replacement
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  return result
    63	}
    64	
    65	function expand (options) {
    66	  // for use with progressive expansion
    67	  const runningParsed = {}
    68	
    69	  let processEnv = process.env
    70	  if (options && options.processEnv != null) {
    71	    processEnv = options.processEnv
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  // dotenv.config() ran before this so the assumption is process.env has already been set
    75	  for (const key in options.parsed) {
    76	    let value = options.parsed[key]
    77	
    78	    // short-circuit scenario: process.env was already set prior to the file value
    79	    if (processEnv[key] && processEnv[key] !== value) {
    80	      value = processEnv[key]
    81	    } else {
    82	      value = expandValue(value, processEnv, runningParsed)
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    options.parsed[key] = _resolveEscapeSequences(value)
    86	
    87	    // for use with progressive expansion
    88	    runningParsed[key] = _resolveEscapeSequences(value)
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  for (const processKey in options.parsed) {
    92	    processEnv[processKey] = options.parsed[processKey]
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  return options
    96	}
    97	
    98	module.exports.expand = expand
    99

     2	import consola, { LogLevels, LogType } from 'consola';
     3	import { filterTruthy, toArray } from '../core/utils/arrays';
     4	import { printHeader } from '../core/utils/log';
     5	import { formatDuration } from '../core/utils/time';
     6	import { ValidationError } from '../core/utils/validation';
     7	import { registerWxt } from '../core/wxt';
     8	import spawn from 'nano-spawn';
     9	
    10	/**
    11	 * Wrap an action handler to add a timer, error handling, and maybe enable debug
    12	 * mode.
    13	 */
    14	export function wrapAction(
    15	  cb: (
    16	    ...args: any[]
    17	  ) => void | { isOngoing?: boolean } | Promise<void | { isOngoing?: boolean }>,
    18	  options?: {
    19	    disableFinishedLog?: boolean;
    20	  },
    21	) {
    22	  return async (...args: any[]) => {
    23	    const level: LogType | undefined = args.find((arg) => arg?.level)?.level;
    24	    if (level && Object.keys(LogLevels).includes(level)) {
    25	      consola.level = LogLevels[level];
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    // Enable consola's debug mode globally at the start of all commands when
    29	    // the `--debug` flag is passed
    30	    const isDebug = !!args.find((arg) => arg?.debug);
    31	    if (isDebug) {
    32	      consola.level = LogLevels.debug;
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    const startTime = Date.now();
    36	    try {
    37	      printHeader();
    38	
    39	      const status = await cb(...args);
    40	
    41	      if (!status?.isOngoing && !options?.disableFinishedLog)
    42	        consola.success(
    43	          `Finished in ${formatDuration(Date.now() - startTime)}`,
    44	        );
    45	    } catch (err) {
    46	      consola.fail(
    47	        `Command failed after ${formatDuration(Date.now() - startTime)}`,
    48	      );
    49	      if (!(err instanceof ValidationError)) {
    50	        consola.error(err);
    51	      }
    52	      process.exit(1);
    53	    }
    54	  };
    55	}
    56	
    57	/**
    58	 * Array flags, when not passed, are either `undefined` or `[undefined]`. This
    59	 * function filters out the
    60	 */
    61	export function getArrayFromFlags<T>(
    62	  flags: any,
    63	  name: string,
    64	): T[] | undefined {
    65	  const array = toArray<T | undefined>(flags[name]);
    66	  const result = filterTruthy(array);
    67	  return result.length ? result : undefined;
    68	}
    69	
    70	const aliasCommandNames = new Set<string>();
    71	/**
    72	 * @param base Command to add this one to
    73	 * @param name The command name to add
    74	 * @param alias The CLI tool being aliased
    75	 * @param bin The CLI tool binary name. Usually the same as the alias
    76	 * @param docsUrl URL to the docs for the aliased CLI tool
    77	 */
    78	export function createAliasedCommand(
    79	  base: CAC,
    80	  name: string,
    81	  alias: string,
    82	  bin: string,
    83	  docsUrl: string,
    84	) {
    85	  const aliasedCommand = base
    86	    .command(name, `Alias for ${alias} (${docsUrl})`)
    87	    .allowUnknownOptions()
    88	    .action(async () => {
    89	      try {
    90	        await registerWxt('build');
    91	
    92	        const args = process.argv.slice(
    93	          process.argv.indexOf(aliasedCommand.name) + 1,
    94	        );
    95	        await spawn(bin, args, {
    96	          stdio: 'inherit',
    97	        });
    98	      } catch {
    99	        // Let the other aliased CLI log errors, just exit
   100	        process.exit(1);
   101	      }
   102	    });
   103	  aliasCommandNames.add(aliasedCommand.name);
   104	}
   105	export function isAliasedCommand(command: Command | undefined): boolean {
   106	  return !!command && aliasCommandNames.has(command.name);
   107	}

     3	import { createHooks } from 'hookable';
     4	import { createWxtPackageManager } from './package-managers';

     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * Global variable set once `createWxt` is called once. Since this variable is
    11	 * used everywhere, this global can be used instead of passing the variable as a
    12	 * function parameter everywhere.
    13	 */
    14	export let wxt: Wxt;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Create and register a global instance of the Wxt interface for use throughout
    18	 * the project.
    19	 */
    20	export async function registerWxt(
    21	  command: WxtCommand,
    22	  inlineConfig: InlineConfig = {},
    23	): Promise<void> {
    24	  // Default NODE_ENV environment variable before other packages, like vite, do it
    25	  // See https://github.com/wxt-dev/wxt/issues/873#issuecomment-2254555523
    26	  process.env.NODE_ENV ??=
    27	    inlineConfig.mode ?? (command === 'serve' ? 'development' : 'production');
    28	
    29	  const hooks = createHooks<WxtHooks>();
    30	  const config = await resolveConfig(inlineConfig, command);
    31	  const [builder, pm] = await Promise.all([
    32	    createViteBuilder(config, hooks, () => wxt.server),
    33	    createWxtPackageManager(config.root),
    34	  ]);
    35	
    36	  wxt = {
    37	    config,
    38	    hooks,
    39	    hook: hooks.hook.bind(hooks),
    40	    get logger() {
    41	      return config.logger;
    42	    },
    43	    async reloadConfig() {
    44	      // Prevent changing the server port when resolving config multiple times
    45	      // get-port-please doesn't always return the same port if it was recently closed.
    46	      if (wxt.config.dev.server?.port) {
    47	        inlineConfig.dev ??= {};
    48	        inlineConfig.dev.server ??= {};
    49	        inlineConfig.dev.server.port = wxt.config.dev.server.port;
    50	      }
    51	
    52	      wxt.config = await resolveConfig(inlineConfig, command);
    53	      await wxt.hooks.callHook('config:resolved', wxt);
    54	    },
    55	    pm,
    56	    builder,
    57	    server: undefined,
    58	  };
    59	
    60	  await initWxtModules();
    61	}
    62	
    63	export async function initWxtModules() {
    64	  // Call setup function and add hooks
    65	  for (const mod of builtinModules) await initWxtModule(mod);
    66	  for (const mod of wxt.config.userModules) await initWxtModule(mod);
    67	
    68	  // Initialize hooks
    69	  wxt.hooks.addHooks(wxt.config.hooks);
    70	
    71	  // Print order for debugging
    72	  if (wxt.config.debug) {
    73	    const order = [
    74	      ...builtinModules.map((module) => module.name),
    75	      ...wxt.config.userModules.map((module) =>
    76	        relative(wxt.config.root, module.id),
    77	      ),
    78	      'wxt.config.ts > hooks',
    79	    ];
    80	    wxt.logger.debug('Hook execution order:');

   627	  const localModules = await Promise.all<WxtModuleWithMetadata<any>>(
   628	    localModulePaths.map(async (file) => {
   629	      const absolutePath = normalizePath(path.resolve(modulesDir, file));
   630	      const { config } = await loadConfig<WxtModule<any>>({
   631	        configFile: absolutePath,
   632	        globalRc: false,
   633	        rcFile: false,
   634	        packageJson: false,
   635	        envName: false,
   636	        dotenv: false,
   637	      });
   638	      if (config == null)
   639	        throw Error(
   640	          `No config found for ${file}. Did you forget to add a default export?`,
   641	        );
   642	      // Add name based on filename
   643	      config.name ??= file;
   644	      return {
   645	        ...config,
   646	        type: 'local',
   647	        id: absolutePath,
   648	      };
   649	    }),
   650	  );

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/repro-env-submit.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TMP=$(mktemp -d)
cleanup() { rm -rf "$TMP"; }
trap cleanup EXIT
cd "$TMP"
printf 'CHROME_EXTENSION_ID=chrome-from-dotenv\nFIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID=firefox-from-dotenv\n' > .env
# create dummy zips so publish-browser-extension includes chrome/firefox config and validates IDs
: > chrome.zip
: > firefox.zip
unset CHROME_EXTENSION_ID FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID
node /testbed/packages/wxt/bin/wxt.mjs submit --dry-run --chrome-zip chrome.zip --firefox-zip firefox.zip 2>&1 | tee output.log
if grep -q 'Missing required config: CHROME_EXTENSION_ID, FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID' output.log; then
  echo 'REPRODUCED: .env was not loaded into process.env'
  exit 42
fi
if grep -q 'Missing required config: CHROME_CLIENT_ID' output.log || grep -q 'Missing required config: .*CHROME_CLIENT_ID' output.log; then
  echo 'FIXED: extension IDs were loaded from .env; validation progressed to other required config'
  exit 0
fi
# If no missing config because dry-run got further, also OK for this reproduction.
echo 'No missing extension ID error found'
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro-env-submit.sh
/tmp/repro-env-submit.sh; status=$?; echo exit=$status; exit 0

import { mkdtempSync, writeFileSync, rmSync } from 'node:fs';
import { tmpdir } from 'node:os';
import { join } from 'node:path';

const tmp = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), 'wxt-env-repro-'));
const cwd = process.cwd();
try {
  process.chdir(tmp);
  writeFileSync('.env', 'CHROME_EXTENSION_ID=chrome-from-dotenv\nFIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID=firefox-from-dotenv\n');
  delete process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID;
  delete process.env.FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID;

  const { loadEnv } = await import('/testbed/packages/wxt/src/core/utils/env.ts');
  const parsed = loadEnv('production', 'chrome');
  console.log('parsed:', parsed);
  console.log('process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID:', process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID);
  if (process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID !== 'chrome-from-dotenv') {
    console.error('REPRODUCED: loadEnv parsed .env but did not populate process.env');
    process.exit(42);
  }
  console.log('FIXED: .env is populated into process.env');
} finally {
  process.chdir(cwd);
  rmSync(tmp, { recursive: true, force: true });
}
EOF

import { readFileSync, existsSync } from 'node:fs';
import { parseEnv } from 'node:util';
import { expand } from 'dotenv-expand';
import type { TargetBrowser } from '../../types';

/** Load environment files based on the current mode and browser. */
export function loadEnv(mode: string, browser: TargetBrowser) {
  const envFiles = [
    // List is ordered with general files first, specific ones last, so the more
    // specific files override the more general ones in the loop below.
    `.env`,
    `.env.local`,
    `.env.${mode}`,
    `.env.${mode}.local`,
    `.env.${browser}`,
    `.env.${browser}.local`,
    `.env.${mode}.${browser}`,
    `.env.${mode}.${browser}.local`,
  ];

  const parsed = Object.fromEntries<string>(
    envFiles.flatMap((filePath) => {
      if (!existsSync(filePath)) return [];

      try {
        const content = readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
        const parsedEnv = parseEnv(content);
        return Object.entries(parsedEnv) as [string, string][];
      } catch {
        return [];
      }
    }),
  );

  // Populate `process.env` so CLIs and config files can read values from `.env`
  // the same way they would after importing `dotenv/config`.
  expand({
    parsed,
    processEnv: process.env as Record<string, string>,
  });

  return parsed;
}
import { existsSync, readFileSync } from "node:fs";
import { parseEnv } from "node:util";
import { expand } from "dotenv-expand";
//#region src/core/utils/env.ts
/** Load environment files based on the current mode and browser. */
function loadEnv(mode, browser) {
        const envFiles = [
                `.env`,
                `.env.local`,
                `.env.${mode}`,
                `.env.${mode}.local`,
                `.env.${browser}`,
                `.env.${browser}.local`,
                `.env.${mode}.${browser}`,
                `.env.${mode}.${browser}.local`
        ];
        const parsed = Object.fromEntries(envFiles.flatMap((filePath) => {
                if (!existsSync(filePath)) return [];
                try {
                        const parsedEnv = parseEnv(readFileSync(filePath, "utf-8"));
                        return Object.entries(parsedEnv);
                } catch {
                        return [];
                }
        }));
        expand({
                parsed,
                processEnv: process.env
        });
        return parsed;
}
//#endregion
export { loadEnv };

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TMP=$(mktemp -d)
cleanup() { rm -rf "$TMP"; }
trap cleanup EXIT
cd "$TMP"
printf 'CHROME_EXTENSION_ID=chrome-from-dotenv\nFIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID=firefox-from-dotenv\n' > .env
: > chrome.zip
: > firefox.zip
unset CHROME_EXTENSION_ID FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID
set +e
node /testbed/packages/wxt/bin/wxt-publish-extension.mjs --dry-run --chrome-zip chrome.zip --firefox-zip firefox.zip > output.log 2>&1
status=$?
set -e
cat output.log
if grep -q 'Missing required config: .*CHROME_EXTENSION_ID' output.log || grep -q 'Missing required config: .*FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID' output.log; then
  echo 'FAIL: .env extension IDs were not loaded into process.env'
  exit 1
fi
if grep -q 'Missing required config:' output.log; then
  echo 'PASS: .env extension IDs were loaded; validation progressed to other missing credentials'
  exit 0
fi
exit "$status"
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro-env-submit.sh

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/check-loadenv-edge.mjs <<'EOF'
import { mkdtempSync, writeFileSync, rmSync } from 'node:fs';
import { tmpdir } from 'node:os';
import { join } from 'node:path';
const tmp = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), 'wxt-env-edge-'));
const cwd = process.cwd();
try {
  process.chdir(tmp);
  writeFileSync('.env', 'BASE=from-file\nEXPANDED=$BASE-suffix\nEXISTING=file\n');
  process.env.EXISTING = 'shell';
  delete process.env.BASE;
  delete process.env.EXPANDED;
  const { loadEnv } = await import('/testbed/packages/wxt/src/core/utils/env.ts');
  loadEnv('production', 'chrome');
  console.log({ BASE: process.env.BASE, EXPANDED: process.env.EXPANDED, EXISTING: process.env.EXISTING });
  if (process.env.BASE !== 'from-file') throw new Error('BASE not loaded');
  if (process.env.EXPANDED !== 'from-file-suffix') throw new Error('EXPANDED not expanded');
  if (process.env.EXISTING !== 'shell') throw new Error('Existing env overwritten');
} finally {
  process.chdir(cwd);
  rmSync(tmp, { recursive: true, force: true });
  delete process.env.EXISTING;
  delete process.env.BASE;
  delete process.env.EXPANDED;
}
EOF

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/repro-loadenv.mjs <<'EOF'
import { mkdtempSync, writeFileSync, rmSync } from 'node:fs';
import { tmpdir } from 'node:os';
import { join } from 'node:path';

const tmp = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), 'wxt-env-repro-'));
const cwd = process.cwd();
try {
  process.chdir(tmp);
  writeFileSync('.env', 'CHROME_EXTENSION_ID=chrome-from-dotenv\nFIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID=firefox-from-dotenv\n');
  delete process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID;
  delete process.env.FIREFOX_EXTENSION_ID;

  const { loadEnv } = await import('/testbed/packages/wxt/src/core/utils/env.ts');
  loadEnv('production', 'chrome');
  console.log('process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID:', process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID);
  if (process.env.CHROME_EXTENSION_ID !== 'chrome-from-dotenv') {
    console.error('REPRODUCED: loadEnv parsed .env but did not populate process.env');
    process.exit(42);
  }
  console.log('FIXED: .env is populated into process.env');
} finally {
  process.chdir(cwd);
  rmSync(tmp, { recursive: true, force: true });
}
EOF
